3|40|shrk_pp_advanced_current|chewable_flag|BOOL|0|A flag denoting if the poison pill is chewable. Chewable poison pills provide that certain types of qualified offers, regardless of whether approved by the board, require the pill to be redeemed, either automatically or by a stockholder vote.
3|41|shrk_pp_advanced_current|min_amend_trigger_flag|BOOL|0|A flag denoting if the poison pill includes a provision in the amendment section of the rights agreement that provides that the board can reduce the trigger thresholds of the poison pill to as low as a specified percentage (usually 10 percent) at any time prior to a person acquiring a percent of company stock equal to the lowered threshold.
